# <a name="office-365-education"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-105">Office 365 教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-105">Office 365 Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p102">Microsoft Office 365 位于不同的计划为了最好地满足组织的需求。如果您正在寻找 Office 365 教育版计划之间的差异，本文将显示在每个包括了哪些功能。Office 365 与基于云的版本的 Microsoft 的下一代通信和协作服务结合使用熟悉的 Microsoft Office 桌面套件 — 包括 Microsoft Exchange Online、 Microsoft SharePoint Online、 Office Online 和Microsoft Skype 业务 online — 可帮助用户从任意虚拟地点通过 Internet 工作效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p102">Microsoft Office 365 is available in a variety of plans to best meet the needs of your organization. If you're looking for the differences between the Office 365 education plans, this article will show you which features are included in each of them. Office 365 combines the familiar Microsoft Office desktop suite with cloud-based versions of Microsoft's next-generation communications and collaboration services—including Microsoft Exchange Online, Microsoft SharePoint Online, Office Online, and Microsoft Skype for Business Online—to help users be productive from virtually anywhere through the Internet.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p103">本文列出了 Office 365 教育版计划 （A1，A3 和 A5） 的功能。若要跨业务和企业计划比较功能，请参阅[业务计划比较 Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=799177) ，或功能的更详细列表，请参阅[Office 365 服务说明](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/jj819284.aspx)在相关服务说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p103">This article lists the features for Office 365 education plans (A1, A3, and A5). To compare features across business and enterprise plans, see [Compare Office 365 for Business plans](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=799177) or, for a more detailed list of features, see the relevant service description at [Office 365 Service Descriptions](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/jj819284.aspx).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-111">若要搜索的支持文章和信息，请参阅[Office 帮助和培训](https://support.office.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-111">To search for support articles and information, see [Office Help and Training](https://support.office.com/).</span></span>
  
## <a name="service-availability-for-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-112">每个计划的服务可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-112">Service availability for each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p104">每个 Office 365 教育版计划包括大量的单个服务，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表显示了每个 Office 365 计划中可用的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p104">Each Office 365 education plan includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>

## <a name="office-365-security-amp-compliance-center-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-627">Office 365 安全性&amp;合规性中心功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-627">Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-628"><a name="SCC"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-628"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p109">[Office 365 安全性&amp;合规性中心](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=824876)旨在帮助您管理跨 Office 365 组织的合规性功能。指向现有 SharePoint 和 Exchange 合规性功能聚集跨 Office 365 的起来的合规性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p109">The [Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=824876) is designed to help you manage compliance features across Office 365 for your organization. Links to existing SharePoint and Exchange compliance features bring together compliance capabilities across Office 365.</span></span> 
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p110">目前，许多合规性功能仍通过进行访问特定于服务的管理界面，如 Exchange 管理员中心 (EAC)。但是，这将在以后更改多个独立于服务的合规性功能添加到安全&amp;合规性中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p110">Currently, many of the compliance features are still accessible through service-specific management interfaces, such as the Exchange admin center (EAC). However, this will change in the future as more service-independent compliance features are added to the Security &amp; Compliance Center.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p111"><sup>1</sup>数据调控使用户能够创建、 发布和手动将标签应用于文档;使用驱动器传送或通过网络; 导入数据创建并应用保留/删除策略跨工作负荷、 用户和组。应用于邮箱的保留策略要求 Office 365 企业版 E3 或 E5。> <sup>2</sup>高级的数据调控，可以保留的重要信息，并通过分类基于和 / 或保留或删除的策略的信息中删除并不重要信息。它包括自动智能/推荐策略; 例如的操作自动将标签应用于数据;应用标签基于敏感数据类型或查询;和使用智能的导入筛选器。它还包括查看员工通信的安全性和合规性目的的监督功能。> <sup>3</sup> unlimited。> <sup>4</sup>高级电子数据展示在美国和西欧 （荷兰） 区域中受支持。（从加拿大和亚太地区客户数据导出到美国。从欧洲、 中东和非洲客户数据导出到西欧 [荷兰]。）> <sup>5</sup>高级的威胁保护也可在 Office 365 A5 作为独立的服务的 Office 365 A1 和 Office 365 A3。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p111"><sup>1</sup> Data governance enables users to create, publish, and manually apply labels to documents; import data using drive shipping or over the network; and create and apply retention/deletion policies across workloads, users, and groups. Retention policies applied to mailboxes require Office 365 Enterprise E3 or E5. > <sup>2</sup> Advanced data governance allows you to retain important information and delete unimportant information by classifying information based on a retention or deletion policy or both. It includes intelligent/automated actions such as recommending policies; automatically applying labels to data; applying labels based on sensitive data types or queries; and use of smart import filters. It also includes the Supervision feature for reviewing employee communications for security and compliance purposes. > <sup>3</sup> Unlimited. > <sup>4</sup> Advanced eDiscovery is supported in the United States and in the Western Europe (Netherlands) region. (Customer data from Canada and Asia Pacific is exported to the United States. Customer data from Europe, the Middle East, and Africa is exported to Western Europe [Netherlands].) > <sup>5</sup> Advanced Threat Protection is available in Office 365 A5 and as a standalone service for Office 365 A1 and Office 365 A3.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]

The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online. Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features. A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user. For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Clients for Skype for Business Online](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx). > <sup>3</sup> Some schools are eligible for Education Plus, which includes Office 365 ProPlus, and allows students, faculty and staff to install the latest version of Office on up to five PC or Mac computers and on other mobile devices, including Windows tablets and the iPad. Schools qualify for Office 365 Education Plus when they license Office institution-wide for faculty and staff through Enrollment for Education Solutions, Open Value Subscription Education Solutions, or a school contract. Note that Access and Publisher are available on PCs only. OneNote for Mac is available as a separate download from the Mac App Store. > <sup>4</sup> Office Online versions are included. ## <a name="office-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-910">Office Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-910">Office Online features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-911"><a name="OfcOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-911"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p113">下表提供了指向 Office 365 教育版计划和功能丰富 Microsoft Office 桌面应用程序中可用的 Office Online 功能功能的比较。使用比较发现 Office Online 中提供了哪些功能，然后单击功能名称以阅读有关该功能的工作原理的简要说明。您可能会发现您的组织中的某些人员可能需要 Excel 桌面应用程序的高级图表功能，而其他人可能只需要查看和宽松编辑 Word 文档和 PowerPoint 演示文稿 with Office Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p113">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office Online feature capabilities available in Office 365 education plans to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps. Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office Online and then click on the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works. You may discover that some people in your organization may need the advanced charting capability of the Excel desktop app while others may only need to view and lightly edit Word documents and PowerPoint presentations with Office Online.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
>  <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p114">仅选择了数量有限的 Office 功能来代表 Office 桌面套件的高级功能。这些表格并未列出全部 Microsoft Office 功能。 >  Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus 是最新 Office 桌面套件的按月订购产品。 >  如果 Microsoft Office Online Server 本地客户已购买 Office 桌面套件许可证（如 Office Professional Plus、Office Standard 或 Office 365 ProPlus 许可证），可以获得 Office Online 编辑许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p114">A limited selection of Office features has been chosen to represent the advanced capabilities of the Office desktop suite. The tables are not a comprehensive list of Microsoft Office features. >  Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus is a monthly subscription offer of the latest Office desktop suite. >  Microsoft Office Online Server on-premises customers get an Office Online editing license if they have purchased an Office desktop suite license (such as an Office Professional Plus, Office Standard, or Office 365 ProPlus license).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p115"><sup>1</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是一款本地服务器，必须购买并管理单独，以便启用支持的 IRM 功能。> <sup>2</sup>传输规则组成的灵活的条件，使您能够定义条件和例外和操作执行基于条件。可用条件和操作 Exchange Online 和 Microsoft Exchange Server 2013 之间的不同。有关可用条件和操作的列表，请参阅的对应条件和每个产品的操作主题。> <sup>3</sup> Exchange Server 2013 使用只有 Microsoft 反恶意软件引擎。Exchange Online 使用多个反恶意软件引擎来扫描入站、 出站和内部邮件的恶意软件。> <sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online 必须包含在 Office 365 订阅计划。> 支持 POP 和 IMAP 帐户，但禁用 Outlook.com (Hotmail) <sup>5</sup>已连接的帐户。> 不支持<sup>6</sup>使用 cmdlet 以使用的地址列表和全局地址列表。> <sup>7</sup>一些第三方 web 部件和加载项可能不可用。> <sup>8</sup>电子数据展示，您需要在本地与云的一个单独的查询。> <sup>9</sup>表指示客户端是否处理关联的计划。并不表示客户端一定要包括在这些计划购买。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p115"><sup>1</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features. > <sup>2</sup> Transport rules are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions and exceptions, and actions to take based on the criteria. The available criteria and actions differ between Exchange Online, and Microsoft Exchange Server 2013. For a list of available criteria and actions, see the corresponding criteria and actions topics for each product. > <sup>3</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine. Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware. > <sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online must be included in the Office 365 subscription plan. > <sup>5</sup> Connected accounts are supported for POP and IMAP accounts, but disabled for Outlook.com (Hotmail). > <sup>6</sup> Using a cmdlet to work with the Address List and Global Address List is not supported. > <sup>7</sup> Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available. > <sup>8</sup> For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud. > <sup>9</sup> Table indicates whether the client works with the associated plans. ### <a name="exchange-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1366">Exchange Online 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1366">Exchange Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1367">查找各个服务方面的 Exchange Online 限制，包括通讯簿限制、邮箱存储空间限制以及报告和邮件跟踪限制等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1367">Find the Exchange Online limits for a variety of service areas, including address book limits, mailbox storage limits, and reporting and message trace limits, to name just a few.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]

> [!IMPORTANT]

When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers. >  You can't modify most of these limits, but you and your users should be aware of them. >  These limits apply to both internal and external recipients. >  By default, Exchange Online Protection (EOP) protects Exchange Online mailboxes. #### <a name="address-book-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1391">通讯簿限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1391">Address book limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1392"><a name="abl"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1392"></span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p118">**地址列表限制** 在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 组织中可以创建的地址列表最大数量。此数目包括 Exchange Online 中的默认地址列表，如"所有联系人"和"所有组"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p118">**Address list limit** The maximum number of address lists that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization. This number includes the default address lists in Exchange Online, such as All Contacts and All Groups.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1395">**脱机通讯簿限制** 在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 组织中可以创建的脱机通讯簿 (OAB) 最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1395">**Offline address book limit** The maximum number of offline address books (OAB) that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1396">**通讯簿策略限制** 在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 组织中可以创建的通讯簿策略 (ABP) 最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1396">**Address book policies limit** The maximum number of address book policies (ABP) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1397">**全局地址列表** 在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 组织中可以创建的全局地址列表 (GAL) 最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1397">**Global address lists** The maximum number of global address lists (GAL) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span>

#### <a name="mailbox-storage-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1418">邮箱存储限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1418">Mailbox storage limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1419"><a name="StorageLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1419"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p119">可用邮箱存储量由邮箱类型和用户的订阅许可证决定。管理员可以减小每位用户或全局的最大邮箱大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p119">The amount of mailbox storage available is determined by the mailbox type and the user's subscription license. Administrators can reduce maximum mailbox sizes per user or globally.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p120">不允许使用日记、传输规则或自动转发规则将邮件复制到 Exchange Online 邮箱中来进行存档。用户的存档邮箱只供该用户使用。Microsoft 保留拒绝在用户存档邮箱用于存储其他用户存档数据的情况下进行无限制存档的权利。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p120">Using journaling, transport rules, or auto-forwarding rules to copy messages to an Exchange Online mailbox for the purposes of archiving is not permitted. A user's archive mailbox is intended for just that user. Microsoft reserves the right to deny unlimited archiving in instances where a user's archive mailbox is used to store archive data for other users.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1445">网站邮箱<sup>4</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1445">Site mailboxes<sup>4</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1446">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1446">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1447">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1447">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1448">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1448">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1449">公用文件夹邮箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1449">Public folder mailboxes</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1450">50 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1450">50 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1451">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1451">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1452">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1452">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1453">组邮箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1453">Group mailboxes</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1454">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1454">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1455">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1455">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1456">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1456">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p121"><sup>1</sup>每个用户最初在存档邮箱中接收 100 GB 的存储。自动扩展存档打开时，达到 100 GB 存储容量时，会自动添加额外的存储空间。有关详细信息，请参阅 Overview of Office 365 中的无限制存档。请参阅 Office 365 路线图有关可用性的详细信息。> <sup>2</sup>访问共享的邮箱，用户必须具有一个 Exchange Online 的许可证。共享的邮箱不需要单独的许可证。但是，如果您想要启用就地存档或共享邮箱置于就地保留或诉讼保留，则 Exchange Online 计划 2 许可证或 Exchange Online 计划 1 与 Exchange Online Archiving 许可证是需要。如果您启用就地存档和自动扩展共享邮箱的存档，达到存档邮箱的 100 GB 存储容量时，会自动添加额外的存储空间。> <sup>3</sup>资源邮箱不需要许可证。> <sup>4</sup>站点邮箱的创建和管理 SharePoint Online 中。有关详细信息，请参阅使用 Office 365 中的站点邮箱准备。> <sup>5</sup>您和被限制为 1000年公用文件夹邮箱，所有公用文件夹邮箱的最大总大小为 50 TB。> <sup>6</sup>就地存档仅可用于存档的已应用许可证为单个用户或实体 （如共享邮箱） 的邮件。使用就地存档作为一种存储来自多个用户或实体的邮件已被禁止。例如，IT 管理员不能创建共享的邮箱，并让用户将其用于存档的显式目的 （通过抄送或密件抄送字段中，或通过传输规则） 复制。请注意多个联系人使用共享的邮箱不实际存储这些单个用户的电子邮件。多个用户具有访问权限，并为共享邮箱发送电子邮件。因此，仅存储在共享邮箱的电子邮件那些发送到或来自，为共享邮箱。> <sup>7</sup>如果您已在 Exchange Online 中创建保留策略，消息将自动移动到用户的存档邮箱仅用户的主邮箱是否大于 10 MB。小于 10 MB 的邮箱，将保留策略将不会自动运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p121"><sup>1</sup> Each user initially receives 100 GB of storage in the archive mailbox. When auto-expanding archiving is turned on, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity is reached. For more information, see Overview of unlimited archiving in Office 365. See the Office 365 Roadmap for details about availability. > <sup>2</sup> To access a shared mailbox, a user must have an Exchange Online license. Shared mailboxes don't require a separate license. However, if you want to enable In-Place Archive or put an In-Place Hold or a Litigation Hold on a shared mailbox, then an Exchange Online Plan 2 license or an Exchange Online Plan 1 with Exchange Online Archiving license is required. If you enable In-Place Archive and auto-expanding archiving for a shared mailbox, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity for the archive mailbox is reached. > <sup>3</sup> Resource mailboxes don't require a license. > <sup>4</sup> Site mailboxes are created and managed in SharePoint Online. For more information, see Prepare for using site mailboxes in Office 365. > <sup>5</sup> You are limited to 1000 public folder mailboxes, and the maximum total size of all public folder mailboxes is 50 TB. > <sup>6</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity (such as a shared mailbox) for which a license has been applied. Using an In-Place Archive as a means of storing mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited. For example, an IT administrator can't create a shared mailbox and have users copy it (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) for the explicit purpose of archiving. Note that a shared mailbox that multiple people use does not actually store email for those individual users. Multiple users have access, and they send email as the shared mailbox. Therefore, the only emails stored in the shared mailbox are those sent to or from it, as the shared mailbox. > <sup>7</sup> If you have created a retention policy in Exchange Online, messages will be automatically moved to a user's archive mailbox only if the user's primary mailbox is larger than 10 MB. The retention policy will not run automatically for mailboxes that are smaller than 10 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="capacity-alerts"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1477">容量报警</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1477">Capacity alerts</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1478"><a name="CapacityAlerts"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1478"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1479">Exchange Online 将在用户的邮箱接近或达到最大容量时提供三种通知类型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1479">Exchange Online provides three kinds of notifications when a user's mailbox is nearing, or at, capacity:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p122">**警告** 用户收到电子邮件警告，其中指出邮箱正接近最大大小限制。此警告旨在建议用户删除不需要的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p122">**Warning** The user receives an email warning that the mailbox is approaching the maximum size limit. This warning is intended to encourage users to delete unwanted mail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p123">**禁止发送** 达到邮箱大小限制时，用户将收到禁止发送的通知电子邮件。在删除足够邮件以便邮箱低于大小限制之前，用户将无法发送新邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p123">**Prohibit Send** The user receives a prohibit-send notification email when the mailbox size limit is reached. The user cannot send new messages until enough email is deleted to bring the mailbox below the size limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p124">**禁止发送/接收** Exchange Online 将在达到邮箱大小限制时拒绝任何传入邮件，并发送未送达报告 (NDR) 给发件人。发件人可选择稍后尝试重新发送该邮件。若要再次接收邮件，用户必须删除邮件，直到邮箱的使用容量低于大小限制为止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p124">**Prohibit Send/Receive** Exchange Online rejects any incoming mail when the mailbox size limit is reached, and sends a non-delivery report (NDR) to the sender. The sender has the option to try resending the mail later. To receive messages again, the user must delete email until the mailbox is below the size limit.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1487">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1487">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1488">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1488">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1489">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1489">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1490">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1490">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1491">警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1491">Warning</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1492">49 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1492">49 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1493">98 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1493">98 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1494">98 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1494">98 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1495">禁止发送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1495">Prohibit Send</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1496">49.5 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1496">49.5 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1497">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1497">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1498">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1498">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1499">禁止发送/接收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1499">Prohibit Send/Receive</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1500">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1500">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1501">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1501">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1502">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1502">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="mailbox-folder-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1503">邮箱文件夹限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1503">Mailbox folder limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1504"><a name="MailboxFolderLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1504"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p125">这些限制旨在将邮箱限制为在 Exchange Online 中受支持的已知尺寸。这些限制旨在防止文件夹中存在不限数量的邮箱项目，邮箱中存在不限数量的文件夹或 Exchange Online 组织中存在不限数量的公用文件夹。出于实用目的，邮箱文件夹限制实际上不受限制，足以支持大多数迁移到 Exchange Online 的 Exchange Online 邮箱和内部部署邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p125">These limits are intended to limit mailboxes to known dimensions that can be supported in Exchange Online. The goal of these limits is to prevent an infinite number of mailbox items per folder, an infinite number of folders per mailbox, or an infinite number of public folders per Exchange Online organization. For practical purposes, mailbox folder limits are in effect unlimited and sufficient to support most Exchange Online mailboxes and on-premises mailboxes that are migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p126">**每个邮箱文件夹的邮件的最大数量** 为邮箱文件夹指定邮件的最大数量。达到该限制时，将无法传递新邮件或无法将其保存在某个文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p126">**Maximum number of messages per mailbox folder** Specifies the maximum number of messages for a mailbox folder. New messages can't be delivered or saved in a folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p127">**每个邮箱文件夹的邮件数量的警告** 指定 Exchange Online 向邮箱所有者发送警告邮件前邮箱文件夹可以保留的邮件数量。达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p127">**Warning for number of messages per mailbox folder** Specifies the number of messages that a mailbox folder can hold before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p128">**"可恢复邮件"文件夹中的每个文件夹的邮件最大数量** 指定"可恢复邮件"文件夹中每个文件夹可以包含的邮件的最大数量。文件夹超出此限制时，将无法存储新邮件。例如，如果"可恢复邮件"文件夹中的"删除"文件夹超出邮件计数限制，而邮箱所有者试图从邮箱中永久删除邮件，删除将会失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p128">**Maximum number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** Specifies the maximum number of messages that can be contained in each folder in the Recoverable Items folder. When a folder exceeds this limit, it can't store new messages. For example, if the Deletions folder in the Recoverable Items folder has exceeded the message count limit and the mailbox owner attempts to permanently delete items from their mailbox, the deletion will fail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1515">**"可恢复邮件"文件夹中的每个文件夹的邮件数量警告** 指定 Exchange Online 将事件记录到应用程序事件日志前，"可恢复邮件"文件夹中的每个文件夹可以保留的邮件数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1515">**Warning for number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** Specifies the number of messages that each folder in the Recoverable Items folder can hold before Exchange Online logs an event to the application event log.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p129">**每个邮箱文件夹的子文件夹的最大数量** 指定可以在邮箱文件夹中创建的子文件夹的最大数量。达到此限制时，邮箱所有者将不能创建新的子文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p129">**Maximum number of subfolders per mailbox folder** Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder. The mailbox owner won't be able to create a new subfolder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p130">**每个邮箱文件夹的子文件夹数量的警告** 指定 Exchange Online 向邮箱所有者发送警告消息之前，可以在邮箱文件夹中创建的子文件夹数量。达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p130">**Warning for number of subfolders per mailbox folder** Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p131">**最大文件夹层次结构的深度** 指定邮箱的文件夹层次结构中级别的最大数量。达到此限制时，邮箱所有者将无法在邮箱文件夹的文件夹层次结构中创建其他级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p131">**Maximum folder hierarchy depth** Specifies the maximum number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox. The mailbox owner won't be able to create another level in the folder hierarchy of the mailbox folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p132">**文件夹层次结构深度的警告** 指定 Exchange Online 向邮箱所有者发送警告消息之前，可以创建的邮箱文件夹的文件夹层次结构中的级别数量。达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p132">**Warning for folder hierarchy depth** Specifies the number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox folder that can be created before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p133">**公用文件夹最大数** 指定完整公用文件夹层次结构中公用文件夹最大数。达到此限制后，必须删除现有公用文件夹，才可以创建新的公用文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p133">**Maximum number of public folders** Specifies the maximum number of public folders in the complete public folder hierarchy. When this limit is reached, existing public folders must be deleted before new public folders can be created.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p134">**每个公用文件夹的子文件夹的最大数量** 指定可以在公用文件夹中创建的子文件夹的最大数量。当达到此限制时，无法在公用文件夹中创建新的子文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p134">**Maximum number of subfolders per public folder** Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder. New subfolders can't be created in a public folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p135">**每个公用文件夹的子文件夹数量的警告** 指定 Exchange Online 向文件夹所有者发送警告消息之前，可以在公用文件夹中创建的子文件夹数量。如果不存在所有者，则警告消息会发送到具有所有者权限的用户。达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p135">**Warning for number of subfolders per public folder** Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the folder owner. If no owner exists, warning messages are sent to users with Owner permissions. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1531">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1531">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1532">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1532">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1533">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1533">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1534">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1534">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p136"><sup>1</sup>可以发送和接收 150 MB （其中邮件永远不会保留 Office 365 数据中心） 的 Office 365 用户之间的邮件。Office 365 数据中心外部路由的消息将受到其他 33%的翻译编码的增加，在其中案例最大邮件大小为 112 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p136"><sup>1</sup> You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between Office 365 users (where the message never leaves the Office 365 datacenters). Messages that are routed outside of the Office 365 datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="message-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1597">邮件限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1597">Message limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1598"><a name="MessageLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1598"></span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p137">**邮件大小限制** 需要邮件大小限制以防止大型邮件阻止送达其他邮件，并影响所有用户的服务性能。这些限制包括一些附件，并且适用于组织范围的所有邮件（入站、出站和内部）。将不送达超过该限制的邮件，同时发件人将收到未送达报告 (NDR)。尽管可以向上、向下或按每个用户配置邮件大小限制，但管理员仍可以创建传输规则以限制任何单个附件的最大大小。若要了解详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 现在支持更大的电子邮件](https://blogs.office.com/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p137">**Message size limit** Message size limits are necessary to prevent large messages from blocking delivery of other messages and affecting service performance for all users. These limits include attachments, and apply organization-wide to all messages (inbound, outbound, and internal). Messages larger than this limit will not be delivered, and the sender will receive a non-delivery report (NDR). While message size limits can be configured up, down, or on a per-user basis, administrators can also create transport rules to limit the maximum size of any individual attachment. To learn more, see [Office 365 now supports larger email messages](https://blogs.office.com/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/).</span></span>
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1604">某些电子邮件客户端可能具有较低的邮件大小限制，或者可能的值小于 Exchange Online 邮件大小限制单个文件附件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1604">Some email clients may have lower message size limits or may limit the size of an individual file attachment to a value that is less than the Exchange Online message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1605">**主题长度限制** 电子邮件的主题行中允许的文本字符的最大数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1605">**Subject length limit** The maximum number of text characters allowed in the subject line of an email message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p138">**文件附件限制** 电子邮件中允许的最大文件附件数。即使所有文件附件的总大小并不违反邮件大小限制，邮件中允许的附件数量也仍具有限制。限制由多部分邮件限制进行控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p138">**File attachments limit** The maximum number of file attachments allowed in an email message. Even if the total size of all the file attachments doesn't violate the message size limit, there is still a limit on how many attachments are allowed in the message. This limit is controlled by the multipart message limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1609">**文件附件大小限制** 单个附件的最大文件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1609">**File attachment size limit** The maximum file size of a single attachment.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p139">此为单个附件的最大文件大小。个别客户端程序（包括 Outlook Web App）可能会将附件大小限制为低于此最大值。Exchange ActiveSync 不基于个别附件实施附件大小限制。Exchange ActiveSync 邮件的所有附件总大小必须低于邮件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p139">This is the maximum file size of a single attachment. Individual client programs, including Outlook Web App, may limit the size of attachments below this maximum. Exchange ActiveSync does not implement attachment size limits on an individual attachment basis. The total size of all attachments to an Exchange ActiveSync message must be less than the message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p140">**多部分邮件限制** MIME 多部分邮件中允许的邮件正文部分的最大数目。此限制还会控制邮件中允许的文件附件的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p140">**Multipart message limit** The maximum number of message body parts that are allowed in a MIME multipart message. This limit also controls the maximum number of file attachments that are allowed in a message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1616">**邮件嵌入深度限制** 电子邮件中允许的最大转发电子邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1616">**Embedded message depth limit** The maximum number of forwarded email messages that are allowed in an email message.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1645">主题长度限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1645">Subject length limit</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1646">255 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1646">255 characters</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1647">255 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1647">255 characters</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1648">255 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1648">255 characters</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1657">文件附件大小限制 - OWA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1657">File attachment size limit - OWA</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1658">35 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1658">35 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1659">35 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1659">35 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1660">35 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1660">35 MB</span></span>  <br/> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p141"><sup>1</sup> office 365 管理员可以指定自定义 1 MB 和 150 MB 之间限制。但是，您可以发送或接收的邮件的大小也取决于您的电子邮件客户端或解决方案的支持。有关自定义您的组织的最大允许的邮件大小的详细信息，请参阅[Office 365 现在支持较大的电子邮件](https://blogs.office.com/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/)。> <sup>2</sup>可以发送和接收达 150 MB （其中邮件永远不会保留 Office 365 数据中心） 的 Office 365 用户之间的邮件。Office 365 数据中心外部路由的消息将受到其他 33%的翻译编码的增加，在其中案例最大邮件大小为 112 MB。> <sup>3</sup> OWA 消息可能受到编码增加 33%的可能性的帐户和限制可以向 25%小于配置的设置发送的邮件的大小。例如，如果您在自定义您的设置为 100 MB 的最大邮件大小，您可以发送消息不大于 75 MB。> <sup>4</sup>通过 Exchange Online 的消息被移动到 Exchange Online 的大小来计算。Exchange Server 2013 之前的 Exchange 版本可能会报告较小的项目。此限制适用于移动基于的迁移使用任何支持 Exchange 邮箱复制服务。其他迁移方法 （Cutover、 暂存、 IMAP、 PST） 和其他第三方工具受到限制常规的邮件大小限制。> <sup>5</sup>有关 OME 使用新功能，请参阅[设置新的 Office 365 邮件加密功能构建到 Azure 信息保护的顶部](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Set-up-new-Office-365-Message-Encryption-capabilities-built-on-top-of-Azure-Information-Protection-7ff0c040-b25c-4378-9904-b1b50210d00e?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p141"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Administrators can specify a custom limit between 1 MB and 150 MB. However, the size of message you can send or receive also depends on what your email client or solution supports. For more information about customizing the maximum allowed message size for your organization, see [Office 365 now supports larger email messages](https://blogs.office.com/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/). > <sup>2</sup> You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between Office 365 users (where the message never leaves the Office 365 datacenters). Messages that are routed outside of the Office 365 datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB. > <sup>3</sup> OWA accounts for the possibility that your message may be subject to the 33% encoding increase and restricts the size of message you can send to 25% less than the configured setting. For example, if you customize your settings for a 100 MB maximum message size, you can send messages no larger than 75 MB. > <sup>4</sup> The size of messages to be moved into Exchange Online are computed by Exchange Online. Versions of Exchange prior to Exchange Server 2013 may report a smaller item size. This limit applies to move based migrations using any supported Exchange Mailbox Replication Service. Other migration methods (Cutover, Staged, IMAP, PST) and other third-party tools are limited by the general message size limit. > <sup>5</sup> For information about OME with new capabilities, see [Set up new Office 365 Message Encryption capabilities built on top of Azure Information Protection](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Set-up-new-Office-365-Message-Encryption-capabilities-built-on-top-of-Azure-Information-Protection-7ff0c040-b25c-4378-9904-b1b50210d00e?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="receiving-and-sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1685">接收和发送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1685">Receiving and sending limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1686"><a name="RecipientLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1686"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p142">接收和发送限制可用于防止出现垃圾邮件和大量邮件蠕虫或病毒。这些限制可以帮助保护系统的运行状况和我们用户的安全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p142">Receiving and sending limits are applied to combat spam and mass-mailing worms or viruses. These limits help to protect the health of our systems and keep our users safe.</span></span>
  
#### <a name="receiving-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1689">接收限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1689">Receiving limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p143">接收限制应用于用户、组或公用文件夹每小时可以接收的邮件数。这适用于从 Internet 和本地服务器收到的邮件。超出接收限制时，只要有电子邮件发送到此邮箱，都会收到未送达报告，指出邮箱已超出最大发送阈值。一个小时后，限制会进行刷新，邮箱将能够再次接收邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p143">Receiving limits apply to the number of messages that a user, group, or public folder can receive per hour. This applies for both messages received from the Internet and from on-premises servers. When the receiving limit has been exceeded, any emails sent to that mailbox will receive a non-delivery report stating that the mailbox has exceeded the maximum delivery threshold. After one hour, the limit will refresh and the mailbox will once again be able to receive messages.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1694">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1694">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1695">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1695">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1696">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1696">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1697">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1697">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |

#### <a name="sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1702">发送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1702">Sending limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1703">发送限制应用于收件人数、邮件数和用户可以从其 Exchange Online 帐户发送的每封邮件的收件人数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1703">Sending limits apply to the number of recipients, number of messages, and number of recipients per message that a user can send from their Exchange Online account.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p144">对于存储在组织的通讯簿中的通讯组，这类组计数为一个收件人。对于存储在邮箱的"联系人"文件夹中的通讯组，单独计数组的各个成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p144">For distribution groups stored in an organization's address book, the group is counted as one recipient. For distribution groups stored in the Contacts folder of a mailbox, the members of the group are counted individually.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p145">**收件人速率限制** 为了阻止送达未经请求的批量邮件，Exchange Online 提供收件人限制以防止用户和应用程序发送大量电子邮件。这些限制适用于每个用户的所有出站和内部邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p145">**Recipient rate limit** To discourage the delivery of unsolicited bulk messages, Exchange Online has recipient limits that prevent users and applications from sending large volumes of email. These limits are applied per-user to all outbound and internal messages.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1708">需要发送合法批量电子邮件的 Exchange Online 客户（例如，客户新闻通讯）应使用专门提供这些服务的第三方提供商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1708">Exchange Online customers who need to send legitimate bulk commercial email (for example, customer newsletters) should use third-party providers that specialize in these services.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1709">**收件人限制** 一封电子邮件的"收件人:"、"抄送:"和"密件抄送:"字段中允许的最大邮件收件人数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1709">**Recipient limit** This is the maximum number of recipients allowed in the To:, Cc:, and Bcc: fields for a single email message.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p146">出于收件人速率限制和收件人限制的目的，组织共享通讯簿中存储的通讯组作为一个收件人计数。在个人通讯列表中，每个收件人单独计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p146">For the purposes of the recipient rate limit and the recipient limit, a distribution group that is stored in the organization's shared address book counts as one recipient. In a personal distribution list, each recipient is counted separately.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p147">**邮件速率限制** 邮件速率限制确定用户在指定时间段内可以从其 Exchange Online 帐户发送的邮件数。此限制有助于防止单个发件人过多消耗系统资源。如果用户提交邮件的速度超过了通过 SMTP 客户端提交邮件的限制，邮件将被拒绝，并且客户端将需要重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p147">**Message rate limit** Message rate limits determine how many messages a user can send from their Exchange Online account within a specified period of time. This limit helps prevent overconsumption of system resources by a single sender. If a user submits messages at a rate that exceeds the limit via SMTP client submission, the messages will be rejected and the client will need to retry.</span></span>

#### <a name="reporting-and-message-trace-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1735">报告和邮件跟踪限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1735">Reporting and message trace limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1736"><a name="bkmk_Reporting_Message_Trace_Limits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1736"></span></span>

#### <a name="retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1738">保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1738">Retention limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1739"><a name="RetentionLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1739"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1740">这些限制控制可以访问收件箱中特定文件夹中的项目的时间长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1740">These limits control the length of time that items in specific folders in the Inbox can be accessed.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1741">**"已删除邮件"文件夹保留期** 邮件在被自动删除之前可在"已删除邮件"文件夹中保留的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1741">**Deleted Items folder retention period** The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Deleted Items folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1742">**保留期从已删除邮件文件夹**永久删除之前保留从已删除邮件文件夹中删除项目的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1742">**Retention period for items removed from the Deleted Items folder** The maximum numbers of days that items removed from the Deleted Items folder are retained before they're permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1743">**"垃圾邮件"文件夹保留期** 邮件在被自动删除之前可在"垃圾邮件"文件夹中保留的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1743">**Junk Email folder retention period** The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Junk Email folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span>

#### <a name="distribution-group-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1762">通讯组限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1762">Distribution group limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1763"><a name="iDistributionGroupLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1763"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1764">这些限制适用于组织的共享地址簿中的通讯组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1764">These limits apply to distribution groups in your organization's shared address book.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1765">**通讯组成员的最大数目**通讯组扩展后确定总收件人计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1765">**Maximum number of distribution group members** The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p149">**限制向大型通讯组发送邮件** 包含此限制所指定数目的成员的通讯组必须已配置传递管理或邮件审批选项。传递管理选项将指定一个允许向通讯组发送邮件的发件人的列表。邮件审批选项将指定一个或多个必须审批发送到通讯组的所有邮件的审阅人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p149">**Limit sending messages to large distribution groups** Distribution groups that contain the number of members specified by this limit must have delivery management or message approval options configured. Delivery management specifies a list of senders who are allowed to send messages to the distribution group. Message approval specifies one or more moderators who must approve all messages sent to the distribution group.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p150">**大型通讯组的最大邮件大小** 如果将一封邮件发送给 5,000 个收件人或更多收件人，则此邮件的大小不能超出此限制。如果此邮件的大小超出此限制，则不会传递此邮件，并且发件人会收到一份未送达报告 (NDR)。在通讯组扩展后确定总收件人计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p150">**Maximum message size for large distribution groups** If a message is sent to 5,000 or more recipients, the message size can't exceed this limit. If the message size exceeds the limit, the message isn't delivered, and the sender receives a non-delivery report (NDR). The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span>

If you are using Azure AD Connect, that number is 50,000. > <sup>2</sup> This limit also applies to admins.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="journal-transport-and-inbox-rule-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1799">日记、传输和收件箱规则限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1799">Journal, transport, and inbox rule limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1800"><a name="TransportRuleLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1800"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p152">以下列表包含适用于日记规则、传输规则的限制（也称为组织范围规则）以及适用于收件箱规则的限制。收件箱规则由单个用户设置，并适用于该用户邮箱发送和接收的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p152">The following list includes limits that apply to journal rules, transport rules (also known as organization-wide rules), and limits that apply to Inbox rules. Inbox rules are set up by individual users and applied to messages sent and received by the individual user's mailbox.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1803">**最大日记规则数** 组织中可具有的日志规则的最大数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1803">**Maximum number of journal rules** The maximum number of journal rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1804">**最大传输规则数** 组织中可具有的规则的最大数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1804">**Maximum number of transport rules** The maximum number of rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p153">**单个传输规则的最大大小**最大可在单个传输规则中使用的字符数。条件、 例外和操作中使用的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p153">**Maximum size of an individual transport rule** The maximum number of characters that can be used in a single transport rule. The characters are used in the conditions, exceptions, and actions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p154">**所有传输规则中使用的所有正则表达式的字符限制** 组织的所有传输规则条件和例外中的所有正则表达式所使用的字符总数。可具有少量使用长而复杂的正则表达式的规则，也可具有多个使用简单正则表达式的规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p154">**Character limit for all regular expressions used in all transport rules** The total number of characters used by all the regular expressions in all the transport rule conditions and exceptions in the organization. You can have a few rules that use long and complex regular expressions, or you can have many rules that use simple regular expressions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p155">**附件内容的扫描限制** 传输规则条件使你可以检查邮件附件的内容，但只能检查从附件提取的文本中的前 1 MB 内容。1 MB 的限制指的是从附件中提取的文本，而不是附件的文件大小。例如，一个 2 MB 的文件可能包含小于 1 MB 的文本，因此将检查整个文本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p155">**Scanning limits for attachment content** The transport rule conditions enable you to examine the content of message attachments, but only the first 1 MB of the text extracted from an attachment is inspected. This 1 MB limit refers to the text extracted from the attachment, not to the file size of the attachment. For example, a 2 MB file may contain less than 1 MB of text, so all of the text would be inspected</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p156">**所有传输规则向一封邮件添加的收件人的最大数目** 当一封邮件由不同的传输规则使用时，只能向该邮件添加有限数目的收件人。在达到此限制后，不会再向该邮件添加任何其余的收件人。此外，传输规则不能向邮件添加通讯组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p156">**Maximum number of recipients added to a message by all transport rules** When a message is acted on by different transport rules, only a finite number of recipients can be added to the message. After the limit is reached, any remaining recipients aren't added to the message. Also, distribution groups can't be added to a message by a transport rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p157">**转发邮件的收件人限制** 可以为收件箱或包含重定向操作的传输规则配置的收件人的最大数目。如果某个规则配置为将邮件重定向到比此数目多的收件人，则不应用该规则，任何满足该规则条件的邮件将不重定向到该规则中列出的任何收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p157">**Forwardee limit** The maximum number of recipients that can be configured for an inbox or transport rule with a redirecting action. If a rule is configured to redirect a message to more than this number of recipients, the rule won't be applied and any message that satisfies the rule condition won't be redirected to any of the recipients listed in the rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p158">**重定向邮件的次数** 将根据收件箱规则自动重定向、转发或答复邮件的次数。例如，用户 A 有一个根据发件人将邮件重定向到用户 B 的收件箱规则。用户 B 有一个根据主题行中的关键字将邮件转发到用户 C 的收件箱规则。如果某邮件同时满足这两个条件，则由于仅允许一次重定向，该邮件仅发送到用户 B，不会转发到用户 C。在这种情况下，邮件将被丢弃，而不会向用户 B 发送未送达报告 (NDR) 以指明邮件未发送给用户 C。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p158">**Number of times a message is redirected** The number of times a message will be redirected, forwarded, or replied to automatically based on Inbox rules. For example, User A has an Inbox rule that redirects messages to User B, based on the sender. User B has an Inbox rule that forwards messages to User C based on keywords in the subject line. If a message satisfies both of these conditions, the message is only sent to User B; it's not forwarded to User C because only one redirection is allowed. In this case, the message is dropped without sending a non-delivery report (NDR) to User B indicating that the message wasn't delivered to User C.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1822">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1822">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1823">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1823">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1824">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1824">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1825">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1825">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1830">传输规则的最大数目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1830">Maximum number of transport rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1831">300 条规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1831">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1832">300 条规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1832">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1833">300 条规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1833">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1834">单个传输规则的最大大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1834">Maximum size of an individual transport rule</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1835">8 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1835">8 KB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1836">8 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1836">8 KB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1837">8 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1837">8 KB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1838">所有传输规则中使用的所有正则表达式的字符限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1838">Character limit for all regular expressions used in all transport rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1839">20 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1839">20 KB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1840">20 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1840">20 KB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1841">20 KB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1841">20 KB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1842">附件内容的扫描限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1842">Scanning limits for content of attachments</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1843">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1843">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1844">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1844">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1845">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1845">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="moderation-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1858">审阅限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1858">Moderation limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1859"><a name="ModerationLimits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1859"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1860">这些限制将控制用于适用于通讯组和传输规则的邮件审批的审阅设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1860">These limits control the moderation settings that are used for message approval applied to distribution groups and transport rules.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1861">**仲裁邮箱的最大大小** 如果仲裁邮箱超出此限制，则以未送达报告 (NDR) 形式将需要审阅的邮件返回给发件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1861">**Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox** If the arbitration mailbox exceeds this limit, messages that require moderation are returned to the sender in a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p159">**审阅人的最大数量**您可以分配给单个审阅的通讯组或的审阅人的最大数量可以添加到使用单个传输规则的邮件。请注意，不能仲裁人为指定通讯组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p159">**Maximum number of moderators** The maximum number of moderators that you can assign to a single moderated distribution group or that can be added to a message using a single transport rule. Note that you can't specify a distribution group as a moderator.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p160">**等待审阅的邮件的过期时间** 默认情况下，等待审阅的邮件在 2 天后过期。但每 7 天将处理一次已过期的中继邮件。这意味着，中继邮件会在 2 到 9 天内随时过期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p160">**Expiration for messages waiting for moderation** By default, a message waiting for moderation expires after two days. However, the processing of expired moderated messages runs every seven days. This means that a moderated message can expire at any time between two and nine days.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p161">**过期的审阅通知邮件的最大速率** 此限制将设置 1 个小时内过期中继邮件的通知邮件的最大数目。对数据中心内的每个邮箱数据库施加了此限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p161">**Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages** This limit sets the maximum number of notification messages for expired moderated messages in a one-hour period. This limit is placed on each mailbox database in the datacenter.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p162">在使用率较高的时段内，一些发件人可能无法收到已过期的中继邮件的通知邮件。但仍可使用送达报告来发现这些通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p162">During periods of heavy usage, some senders may not receive notification messages for moderated messages that have expired. However, these notifications are still discoverable using delivery reports.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1883">等待审阅的邮件的过期时间</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1883">Expiration for messages waiting for moderation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1884">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1884">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1885">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1885">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1886">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1886">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="exchange-activesync-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1891">Exchange ActiveSync 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1891">Exchange ActiveSync limits</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1892"><a name="bkmk_ExchangeActiveSync_Limits"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1892"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1893">以下限制适用于 Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync，一个在移动设备和 Exchange 之间同步邮箱数据的客户端协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1893">The following limits apply to Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, a client protocol that synchronizes mailbox data between mobile devices and Exchange.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1894">**Exchange ActiveSync 设备限制** 每个邮箱中的 Exchange ActiveSync 设备的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1894">**Exchange ActiveSync device limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices per mailbox.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1895">**Exchange ActiveSync 设备删除限制** Exchange 管理员在一个月内可删除的 Exchange ActiveSync 设备的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1895">**Exchange ActiveSync device deletion limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices that an Exchange administrator can delete in a single month.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1896">**Exchange ActiveSync 文件附件限制** Exchange ActiveSync 设备可以发送或接收的消息文件附件的最大大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1896">**Exchange ActiveSync file attachment limit** The maximum size of a message file attachment that can be sent or received by an Exchange ActiveSync device.</span></span>

## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1913">OneDrive for Business 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1913">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1914"><a name="OfcOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1914"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p163">OneDrive for Business (以前称为 SkyDrive Pro) 是在云中的个人联机存储空间。使用它来存储工作文件跨多个设备具有易用性和安全性。根据需要与同事共享您的文件和编辑 Office 文档的实时 with Office Online 在一起。同步到本地计算机使用 OneDrive for Business 同步应用程序的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p163">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud. Use it to store your work files across multiple devices with ease and security. Share your files with colleagues as needed, and edit Office documents together in real time with Office Online. Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync app.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p164">OneDrive for Business 包含 SharePoint Online 中，还可以作为独立计划购买。OneDrive for Business 独立选项包括 Office Online。若要了解详细信息，请参阅[OneDrive for Business 是什么？](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271073)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p164">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan. The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office Online. To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271073)</span></span>
  
### <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1922">系统要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1922">System Requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p165">OneDrive for Business 同步客户端具有比 OneDrive 客户端的不同的系统要求。若要了解详细信息，请参阅[如何安装 OneDrive for Business 同步客户端](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p165">The OneDrive for Business sync client has different system requirements than the OneDrive client. To learn more, see [How to install the OneDrive for Business sync client](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span></span>
  
### <a name="onedrive-for-business-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1925">OneDrive for Business 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1925">OneDrive for Business limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1926">OneDrive for Business 计划 1 提供 1 TB 的每个用户的存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1926">OneDrive for Business Plan 1 provides 1 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p166">以下符合条件的计划为至少五个用户的订阅中的每个用户提供无限的 OneDrive 存储空间。 Microsoft 将为每个用户提供 5 TB 的初始存储空间。如果需要额外的 OneDrive 存储空间，客户可以与 Microsoft 支持部门联系，根据需要进行申请。对于少于五个用户的订阅，每个用户可获得 1 TB 的存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p166">The following qualifying plans provide unlimited OneDrive storage per user for subscriptions with at least five users. Microsoft will provide an initial 5 TB of storage space per user. Customers who want additional OneDrive storage can request it as needed by contacting Microsoft Support. Subscriptions with less than five users receive 1 TB of storage per user.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1931">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1931">Office 365 A1</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1932">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1932">Office 365 A3</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1933">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1933">Office 365 A5</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p167">您不能分配给特定 OneDrive 用户的更多的存储。但是，您可以降低用户看到的存储量。Office 365 企业 F1 用户需要更多存储，如果您将需要升级到 Office 365 企业版 E1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p167">You cannot allocate more storage to a specific OneDrive user. However, you can lower the amount of storage that a user sees. If an Office 365 Enterprise F1 user needs more storage, then you'll need to upgrade to Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-1937">有关您无法添加到 OneDrive for Business 的文件类型的信息，请参阅[，无法将添加到列表或库的文件类型](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=273757)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-1937">For information about file types that you can't add to OneDrive for Business, see [Types of files that cannot be added to a list or library](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=273757).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p168">SharePoint Online 中包含的 OneDrive for Business。若要了解有关 SharePoint Online 中的其他限制，如网站集配额、 文件上载限制和存储限制，请参阅[SharePoint Online 的软件边界和限制](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=271273)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p168">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online. To learn about additional limitations in SharePoint Online, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits, see [SharePoint Online software boundaries and limits](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=271273).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p170"><sup>1</sup>到使用文件夹同步，您必须具有 Office 2013 或更高版本 (标准版或 Professional edition) 或 Office 365 订阅包括 Office 应用程序。Office 365 业务 Essentials、 Office 365 企业版 E1，和 Office 365 教育版规划中不包括订阅 Office 桌面应用程序。但是，您可以使用文件夹同步，如果您有 Office 2013 或更高版本安装并订阅这些计划之一。> <sup>2</sup>由于网亭用户不能是管理员，因此包含网亭用户的租户需要至少一个企业用户才能访问管理中心。> <sup>3</sup> SharePoint Online 客户需要下载并安装免费排名模型优化应用程序创建和自定义排名模型。> <sup>4</sup>使用电子数据展示功能时，允许该功能的计划的许可要求适用于所有最终用户的电子数据展示操作 （搜索，保留，导出） 的一部分。> <sup>5</sup>某些提供程序可能会阻止您所在国家/地区。> <sup>6</sup>与组织外部的某个人通过电子邮件中共享文档、 库或网站。管理员执行能够将其打开，但会收到一条警告消息，表明它无法进行共享的文件可访问外部国家/地区。尝试与组织外部的某个人共享的用户将收到相同的警告消息。> <sup>7</sup>可以在任何移动浏览器中查看文档。您需要安装 Office Mobile 应用程序编辑文档。Office Mobile 是当前适用于 Windows phone 和平板电脑、 Android 电话和平板电脑、 iPhone 和 iPad。> <sup>8</sup>帮助是仅可用于简体中文和英语。> 无法添加<sup>9</sup>博客评论。> <sup>10</sup>组织社区网站，但公共提供社区帮助不可用。> <sup>11</sup> access 2010 不支持。> <sup>12</sup>沙盒解决方案不能包含用户代码。他们只能包含定义 (.xml) 文件和激活由服务器处理的资源。> <sup>13</sup> InfoPath 表单包含用户代码 （沙盒） 仅在 InfoPath 富客户端中使用。> <sup>14</sup>经过身份验证 SharePoint Online 用户可以访问与分面导航的专用网站集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p170"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or an Office 365 subscription that includes Office applications. Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Enterprise E1, and Office 365 education plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications. However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans. > <sup>2</sup> Because Kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with Kiosk users need at least one Enterprise user to access the admin center. > <sup>3</sup> SharePoint Online customers need to download and install the free Rank Model Tuning App to create and customize ranking models. > <sup>4</sup> When you use eDiscovery features, the licensing requirement for a plan that permits that feature applies to all end users that are part of the eDiscovery action (Search, Hold, Export). > <sup>5</sup> Some providers may be blocked in your country/region. > <sup>6</sup> Sharing a document, library, or site by email with someone outside of your organization. Administrators do have the ability to turn it on but will get a warning message indicating that it could make files shared accessible outside of your country. Users who attempt to share with someone outside of the organization will receive the same warning message. > <sup>7</sup> You can view documents in any Mobile browser. You need to install the Office Mobile app to edit documents. Office Mobile is currently available for Windows phones and tablets, Android phones and tablets, iPhone, and iPad. > <sup>8</sup> Help is available only in Simplified Chinese and English. > <sup>9</sup> Comments on blogs cannot be added. > <sup>10</sup> Organization community website is available, but public community-provided help is not available. > <sup>11</sup> Access 2010 is not supported. > <sup>12</sup> Sandboxed solutions cannot contain user code. They may only contain definition (.xml) files and resources that are processed by the server when they activate. > <sup>13</sup> InfoPath Forms that contain user code (Sandbox) can only be consumed in InfoPath Rich Client. > <sup>14</sup> Authenticated SharePoint Online users can access private site collections with faceted navigation.</span></span> 
  
### <a name="sharepoint-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-2919">SharePoint Online 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-2919">SharePoint Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-2920">下表显示了每个 Office 365 教育版计划的 SharePoint 限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-2920">The following table shows the SharePoint limits for each Office 365 education plan.</span></span>
  
|||||

> [!NOTE]
> > <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p171"><sup>1</sup>您可以购买其他 SharePoint Online 存储无限的的量。请参阅[更改为您的订阅的存储空间](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Change-storage-space-for-your-subscription-96EA3533-DE64-4B01-839A-C560875A662C?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。> <sup>2</sup>建议监视回收站并定期清空。它使用的存储空间属于组织的总文件存储限制。> <sup>3</sup>后的 Office 365 订阅和 SharePoint Online 独立计划的金额添加存储。> <sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online 管理员可以设置的网站集和网站的存储使用限制。> <sup>5</sup>不包括 OneDrive for Business 网站集为每个许可用户创建。> <sup>6</sup>如果您有 500000 多个用户，请与 Microsoft 代表联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p171"><sup>1</sup> You can purchase an unlimited amount of additional SharePoint Online storage. See [Change storage space for your subscription](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Change-storage-space-for-your-subscription-96EA3533-DE64-4B01-839A-C560875A662C?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US). > <sup>2</sup> We recommend monitoring the Recycle Bin and emptying it regularly. The storage space it uses is part of the organization's total file storage limit. > <sup>3</sup> When you have an Office 365 subscription and a SharePoint Online standalone plan, the storage amounts are added. > <sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online administrators can set storage use limits for site collections and sites. > <sup>5</sup> Not including the OneDrive for Business site collections created for each licensed user. > <sup>6</sup> If you have more than 500,000 users, please contact a Microsoft representative.</span></span>

Lync 2013 Basic is available for all customers. The Lync Basic desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online. Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 A3 include the full Skype for Business (Lync) application, which includes additional features such as advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features. A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user. For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Clients for Skype for Business Online](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx)> <sup>2</sup> You must assign an Exchange Online (Plan 2) plan to users who you want to have voice mail. An Exchange Online (Plan 1) plan can't be used for voice mail.</span></span> 
  
### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3471">Skype 业务 online 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3471">Skype for Business Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3472">Skype 业务 online 中的限制分为以下类别：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3472">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3473">对等限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3473">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3474">会议限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3474">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3475">会议保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3475">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3476">分钟限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3476">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p175">应用于 Office 365 组织的限制会有所不同长组织已注册服务中。限制更改时在 Microsoft 数据中心，它可能需要一些时间，以将更改应用于所有现有客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p175">The limits applied to an Office 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service. When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3479">对等限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3479">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p176">**文件传输限制** 在 Skype for Business Online IM 对话中可以传输的文件大小上限。若要了解哪些类型的文件会被阻止不能进行文件传输，请参阅关于 [在 Skype for Business Online 中发送和接收文件或附件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=398280)的 Microsoft 支持文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p176">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=398280).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3482">**打开选项卡式的对话限制** Skype for Business 用户一次可以打开的对话选项卡的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3482">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>

#### <a name="meeting-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3495">会议限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3495">Meeting limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3496">**文件上载限制** 可以上载到 Skype for Business 会议的文件（包括讲义和 PowerPoint 演示文稿）大小上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3496">**File upload limit** The maximum size of files that can be uploaded to a Skype for Business meeting, including handouts and PowerPoint presentations.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3497">**Skype for Business 会议中的参与者** 一次 Skype for Business 会议的参与者（包括演示者在内）数量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3497">**Participants in a Skype for Business meeting** The maximum number of participants (including the presenter) who can join a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3498">**Skype for Business 会议中的演示者** 一次 Skype for Business 会议中的演示者数量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3498">**Presenters in a Skype for Business meeting** The maximum number of presenters in a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3499">**Skype for Business Web App 会议参与者** 可以参加 Skype for Business Web App 会议的参与者数量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3499">**Skype for Business web app meeting participants** The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3500">**Skype for Business Web App 匿名参与者** 可以匿名参加 Skype for Business Web App 会议的参与者数量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3500">**Skype for Business web app anonymous participants** The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can anonymously join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3501">**来宾通过电话加入** 可以通过电话拨入会议的来宾最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3501">**Guests joining by phone** The maximum number of guests who can call in to a meeting.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-p177"><sup>1</sup>如果 Skype 业务会议中的参与者数目超过 75 参与者，然后在会议名单中的参与者列表 （演示者和与会者） 将被截断，以使单个与会者看到只有演示者和个人与会者的名称。完整参与者列表保持向会议中演示者可见。此外，图库视图和 IM 错误是隐藏的与会者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-p177"><sup>1</sup> If the number of participants in a Skype for Business meeting exceeds 75 participants, then the participant list (presenters and attendees) in the meeting roster will be truncated so that an individual attendee sees only the presenters and the individual attendee's own name. The full participant list remains visible to the presenters in the meeting. Also, Gallery View and IM errors are hidden from the attendees.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3537">会议保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3537">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3538">**会议内容保留期** 最后一个人离开会议后，任何上载的会议内容在永久性删除之前保留在 Skype for Business 中的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3538">**Meeting content retention period** The amount of time after the last person leaves a meeting that any uploaded meeting content is retained in Skype for Business before it is permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3539">**会议有效期** 在会议结束后，用户可访问该会议的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3539">**Meeting expiration period** The amount of time after a meeting has ended that users can access the meeting.</span></span> 
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3540">每个人可以随时在数据库中有 1000年会议的最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3540">Each person can have a maximum of 1000 conferences in the database at any time.</span></span>

#### <a name="minute-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3569">分钟限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3569">Minute limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="aaa7a-3570">有关 minute 限制 Skype 业务联机国内和国际呼叫计划的信息，请参阅[Skype 业务联机 PSTN 服务使用的术语](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Skype-for-Business-Online-PSTN-services-use-terms-dc6e95cd-51e8-49ca-bcd3-78dc9dae486a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aaa7a-3570">For information about minute limitations in Skype for Business Online Domestic and International Calling Plans, see [Skype for Business Online PSTN services use terms](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Skype-for-Business-Online-PSTN-services-use-terms-dc6e95cd-51e8-49ca-bcd3-78dc9dae486a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span>
